\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ deque\ (pronounced\ "{}deck"{})\ is\ a\ double-\/ended\ queue,\ though\ this\ is\ partially\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ a\ misnomer.\ A\ deque\ does\ indeed\ let\ you\ add\ and\ remove\ values\ from\ both\ ends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ the\ container,\ but\ it's\ not\ usually\ used\ for\ such\ a\ thing\ and\ instead\ is\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ a\ more\ flexible\ version\ of\ a\ vector.\ It\ provides\ operator[]\ (random\ access)\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ can\ insert\ items\ anywhere\ and\ not\ just\ at\ the\ front\ and\ back.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ }}

\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ instead\ implemented\ as\ a\ list\ of\ arrays.\ The\ benefit\ of\ this\ is\ that\ memory\ usage\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ lower\ and\ that\ random\ access\ can\ be\ had\ with\ decent\ efficiency.\ }}
